==========================The_first_checker_query=========================
You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// failure case
package xxx;
public class Foo {
    public void bar() {
        String x;
        x = "foo";
        x += "bar";
        x += "baz";
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 1
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 2

```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getText().contains("+=")) {
            ASTAssignableExpr leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                if (variableAccess.getType() != null && variableAccess.getType().isString()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getText().contains("+=")) {
            ASTAssignableExpr leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                String variableName = variableAccess.getName();
                NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.getParent().getParent().descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
                    .filter(assign -> assign.getText().contains("+=") && ((ASTVariableAccess) assign.getLeftOperand()).getName().equals(variableName));
                if (assignments.count() > 1) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getText().equals("+=")) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.firstChild(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getText().equals("x")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getText().contains("+=")) {
            ASTAssignableExpr leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                if (variableAccess.getText().equals("x")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKinds.PLUS_ASSIGN && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getText().equals("+=")) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.firstChild(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getText().equals("x")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

5. Count the number of occurrences where the `+=` operator is used for string concatenation.

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getText().equals("+=")) {
            ASTVariableAccess leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand().firstChild(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (leftOperand != null && leftOperand.getText().equals("x")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getText().equals("+=")) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.firstChild(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getText().equals("x")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {

            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getText().equals("x")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getText().contains("+=")) {
            ASTVariableAccess leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand().firstChild(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (leftOperand != null && leftOperand.getText().equals("x")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getText().equals("+=")) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.firstChild(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getText().equals("x")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isString()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getText().contains("+=")) {
            ASTVariableAccess leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand().firstChild(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (leftOperand != null && leftOperand.getText().equals("x")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getText().contains("+=")) {
            NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.ancestorsOrSelf()
                .filter(ASTBlock.class)
                .first()
                .descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
                .filter(assign -> assign.getText().contains("+="));

            if (assignments.count() > 1) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node)) {
            if (!JavaRuleUtil.isStringBuilderCtorOrAppend(node)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_EQUAL) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getText().equals("result")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQUAL) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            if (infixExpr != null && infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = infixExpr.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getText().equals("result")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

=========================logics=========================
1. Get all assignment expressions in the code.
2. Check whether the assignment expression uses the `+=` operator.
3. Check whether the left-hand side operand of the `+=` operator is a string variable.
4. Check whether the `+=` operator is used more than once in the same scope (e.g., within a loop or method).

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getText().equals("result")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ASSIGN) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            if (infixExpr != null && infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = infixExpr.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getText().equals("result")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKinds.PLUSEQ) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isString()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKinds.EQ) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            if (infixExpr != null && infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKinds.PLUS) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = infixExpr.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isString()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// violation: concat to String in for/while loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    public void bad1() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
        Iterator iter = values.iterator();
        while (iter.hasNext()) {
            logStatement = logStatement + iter.next() + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
    public void bad2() {
        String log = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val1 : values) {
            log += val1; // bad
        }
        for (String val2 : values) log += val2; // bad
    }

    public void bad3() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement += val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 6
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 5

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT || node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isString()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========================The_first_checker_query=========================
You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// violation: concat to String in for/while loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    public void bad1() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
        Iterator iter = values.iterator();
        while (iter.hasNext()) {
            logStatement = logStatement + iter.next() + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
    public void bad2() {
        String log = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val1 : values) {
            log += val1; // bad
        }
        for (String val2 : values) log += val2; // bad
    }

    public void bad3() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement += val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 6
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 5

```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_EQUALS) {
            ASTVariableAccess leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand().firstChild(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (leftOperand != null && leftOperand.getType() != null && leftOperand.getType().isString()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQUALS) {
            ASTInfixExpression rightOperand = node.getRightOperand().firstChild(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            if (rightOperand != null && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(rightOperand)) {
                ASTVariableAccess leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand().firstChild(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (leftOperand != null && leftOperand.getType() != null && leftOperand.getType().isString()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========================The_first_checker_query=========================
You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// violation: concat to String in for/while loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    public void bad1() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
        Iterator iter = values.iterator();
        while (iter.hasNext()) {
            logStatement = logStatement + iter.next() + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
    public void bad2() {
        String log = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val1 : values) {
            log += val1; // bad
        }
        for (String val2 : values) log += val2; // bad
    }

    public void bad3() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement += val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 6
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 5

```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT || node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getType() != null && variableAccess.getType().isString()) {
                ASTBlockStatement blockStatement = node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTBlockStatement.class);
                if (blockStatement != null) {
                    ASTBlock block = blockStatement.getFirstParentOfType(ASTBlock.class);
                    if (block != null) {
                        ASTStatement statement = block.getFirstChildOfType(ASTStatement.class);
                        if (statement != null && (statement.getFirstChildOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null || statement.getFirstChildOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null)) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_EQUAL) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isString()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQUAL) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            if (infixExpr != null && infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = infixExpr.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isString()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// violation: various concats in loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {
    public String bad() {
        String description = " " + ";";
        List<String> persons = new ArrayList<String>();
        for (final String person : persons) {
            if (person != null) {
                description += "0" + ":"; //bad
            } else {
                description += ":"; //bad
            }
            description += person.toString() + ":"; // bad
            description += ";"; // bad
            description += person.toString(); // bad
        }
        return description;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaToken.Operator.PLUS_ASSIGN) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getReferencedSym() != null && varAccess.getReferencedSym().getName().equals("description")) {
                ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
                if (infixExpr != null && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(infixExpr)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                } else if (node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class) != null) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                } else if (node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null) {
                    ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                    if (methodCall.getMethodName().equals("toString")) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;

        List<String> persons = new ArrayList<String>();

            if (person != null) {
                description += "0" + ":"; //bad
            } else {
                description += ":"; //bad
            }
            description += person.toString() + ":"; // bad
            description += ";"; // bad
            description += person.toString(); // bad
        }
        return description;
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaToken.Operator.PLUS_ASSIGN) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isString()) {
                ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
                if (infixExpr != null && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(infixExpr)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN) {
            if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaToken.Operator.PLUS_ASSIGN) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isString()) {
                ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
                if (infixExpr != null && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(infixExpr)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            if (!JavaRuleUtil.isStringBuilderCtorOrAppend(node.getRightOperand())) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            if (node.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess leftOperand = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getLeftOperand();
                if (leftOperand.getType() != null && leftOperand.getType().isString()) {
                    if (!JavaRuleUtil.isStringBuilderCtorOrAppend(node.getRightOperand())) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;

    public void bad() {

        int i = 0;
        do {
            logStatement = logStatement + values.get(i++) + ", "; // bad
        } while (i < values.length());
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKinds.PLUS_ASSIGN || node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKinds.PLUS) {
            ASTExpression rightOperand = node.getRightOperand();
            if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(rightOperand)) {
                ASTVariableAccess leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand().firstChild(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (leftOperand != null && leftOperand.getType() != null && leftOperand.getType().isString()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

If the code uses `+` or `+=` for string concatenation inside a loop and does not use an explicit `StringBuilder` or `StringBuffer`, then this test case violates the rule. 

In this test case:
- The `logStatement = logStatement + values.get(i++) + ", "` line uses the `+` operator for string concatenation.
- The concatenation is inside a `do-while` loop.
- The concatenation is performed multiple times (once per iteration of the loop).
- No explicit `StringBuilder` or `StringBuffer` is used.

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            if (!JavaRuleUtil.isStringBuilderCtorOrAppend(node.getRightOperand())) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == InternalInterfaces.OperatorLike.PLUS_EQUAL) {
            ASTAssignableExpr leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                if (varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isString()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    private String logStatement = "";

    public void bad() {
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKinds.PLUS_ASSIGN || node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKinds.ASSIGN) {
            if (node.getRightOperand() instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = (ASTInfixExpression) node.getRightOperand();
                if (infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKinds.PLUS) {
                    if (infixExpr.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess leftVar = (ASTVariableAccess) infixExpr.getLeftOperand();
                        if (leftVar.getReferencedName().equals("logStatement")) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

// violation: concat to String field in loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    private String logStatement = "";

    public void bad() {
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }

    public void good() {
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder(logStatement);
        for (String val : values) {
            sb.append(val).append(", ");
        }
        logStatement = sb.toString();
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKinds.PLUS_ASSIGN) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getReferencedName().equals("logStatement")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN || node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ASSIGN) {
            if (node.getRightOperand() instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = (ASTInfixExpression) node.getRightOperand();
                if (infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
                    if (infixExpr.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) infixExpr.getLeftOperand();
                        if (varAccess.getReferencedName().equals("logStatement")) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

// violation: concat to String field in loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    private String logStatement = "";

    public void bad() {
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }

    public void good() {
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder(logStatement);
        for (String val : values) {
            sb.append(val).append(", ");
        }
        logStatement = sb.toString();
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getRightOperand() instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = (ASTInfixExpression) node.getRightOperand();
            if (infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
                if (infixExpr.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                    ASTVariableAccess leftVarAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) infixExpr.getLeftOperand();
                    if (leftVarAccess.getReferencedSym() instanceof JVariableSymbol) {
                        JVariableSymbol symbol = (JVariableSymbol) leftVarAccess.getReferencedSym();
                        if (symbol.getType().isString()) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT || node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isString()) {
                if (!JavaRuleUtil.isStringBuilderCtorOrAppend(node)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getText().contains("+=")) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getText().equals("result")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// False positive for assignments
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsFP {
    public void bar() {
        String result;
        result = "a";
        result += "b"; // violation
        result += "c"; // violation
        result = "d"; // FP
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 10
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 2

```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node)) {
            NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.ancestorsOrSelf()
                .filter(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
                .filter(expr -> JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(expr));

            if (assignments.count() > 1) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

If the `+=` operator is used more than once for the same `String` variable, then it violates the rule. Reassigning the `String` variable to a new value (e.g., `result = "d";`) is a false positive and does not violate the rule.

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getType() != null && variableAccess.getType().isString()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            JavaNode leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                if (variableAccess.getType() != null && variableAccess.getType().isString()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========================The_first_checker_query=========================
You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// Test new rule example
public class Foo {
                String inefficientConcatenation() {
                    String result = "";
                    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
                        // warning: this concatenation will create one new StringBuilder per iteration
                        result += getStringFromSomeWhere(i);
                    }
                    return result;
                }

                String efficientConcatenation() {
                    // better would be to use one StringBuilder for the entire loop
                    StringBuilder result = new StringBuilder();
                    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
                        result.append(getStringFromSomeWhere(i));
                    }
                    return result.toString();
                }

                String getStringFromSomeWhere(int i) {
                    return "a" + i;
                }
            }
The description of this test case is: bad 11
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 1

```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaToken.Operator.PLUS_ASSIGN && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node)) {
            ASTBlock block = node.ancestors(ASTBlock.class).first();
            if (block != null) {
                long count = block.descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
                    .filter(expr -> expr.getOperator() == JavaToken.Operator.PLUS_ASSIGN && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(expr))
                    .count();
                if (count > 1) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;

public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaToken.Operator.PLUS_ASSIGN && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node)) {
            ASTBlock block = node.ancestors(ASTBlock.class).first();
            if (block != null) {
                long count = block.descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
                    .filter(expr -> expr.getOperator() == JavaToken.Operator.PLUS_ASSIGN && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(expr))
                    .count();
                if (count > 1) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========================第3轮为第一个测试用例生成checker========================
=========================logics=========================
1. Get all occurrences of the `+=` operator in the code.
2. Check whether the `+=` operator is used for string concatenation.
3. Check whether the `+=` operator is used inside a loop.
4. Get the number of times the `+=` operator is used for string concatenation inside a loop.
5. Check whether the number of occurrences is greater than 1.
6. Check whether a `StringBuilder` or `StringBuffer` is explicitly used for string concatenation in the same context.

If the `+=` operator is used for string concatenation inside a loop more than once and no explicit `StringBuilder` or `StringBuffer` is used, then this test case violates the rule. 

In this test case:
- The `+=` operator is used for string concatenation in the `inefficientConcatenation` method.
- It is used inside a loop.
- It is used more than once (10 times in this case).
- No explicit `StringBuilder` or `StringBuffer` is used in the `inefficientConcatenation` method.

                String inefficientConcatenation() {

                    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
                        // warning: this concatenation will create one new StringBuilder per iteration
                        result += getStringFromSomeWhere(i);
                    }
                    return result;
                }

                String efficientConcatenation() {
                    // better would be to use one StringBuilder for the entire loop
                    StringBuilder result = new StringBuilder();
                    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
                        result.append(getStringFromSomeWhere(i));
                    }
                    return result.toString();
                }

                String getStringFromSomeWhere(int i) {
                    return "a" + i;
                }

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaToken.ADD_ASSIGN && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            ASTBlock block = node.ancestors(ASTBlock.class).first();
            if (block != null) {
                long count = block.descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
                    .filter(expr -> expr.getOperator() == JavaToken.ADD_ASSIGN && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(expr.getRightOperand()))
                    .count();
                if (count > 1) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            ASTBlock block = node.ancestors(ASTBlock.class).first();
            if (block != null) {
                NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = block.descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
                    .filter(expr -> expr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(expr.getRightOperand()));
                if (assignments.count() > 1) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// Test new rule example
public class Foo {
                String inefficientConcatenation() {
                    String result = "";
                    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
                        // warning: this concatenation will create one new StringBuilder per iteration
                        result += getStringFromSomeWhere(i);
                    }
                    return result;
                }

                String efficientConcatenation() {
                    // better would be to use one StringBuilder for the entire loop
                    StringBuilder result = new StringBuilder();
                    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
                        result.append(getStringFromSomeWhere(i));
                    }
                    return result.toString();
                }

                String getStringFromSomeWhere(int i) {
                    return "a" + i;
                }
            }
The description of this test case is: bad 11
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 1

```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaToken.Operator.PLUS_ASSIGN && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node)) {
            ASTBlock block = node.ancestors(ASTBlock.class).first();
            if (block != null) {
                long count = block.descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
                    .filter(expr -> expr.getOperator() == JavaToken.Operator.PLUS_ASSIGN && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(expr))
                    .count();
                if (count > 1) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
